| 0:50:00| Let's get this into the record.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3000)|
| 0:50:04| Whereas, Trees Knoxville is a network of various community organizations and leaders that share a common vision of growing our urban forest.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3004)|
| 0:50:12| And whereas, Trees Knoxville recently received the Urban and Community Forestry Partnership Award from the Southern Group of State Foresters| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3012)|
| 0:50:18| in recognition of the organization's outstanding work in growing partnerships, training volunteers,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3018)|
| 0:50:23| and helping to distribute and plant thousands of trees on public and private lands.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3023)|
| 0:50:27| And whereas, Trees Knoxville began in 2014 with a presentation to the Knoxville Tree Board,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3027)|
| 0:50:32| followed by the formulation of a committee that ultimately recommended that a non-profit be formed| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3032)|
| 0:50:37| to support the city and county's efforts to preserve and enhance the urban forest.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3037)|
| 0:50:41| And whereas, Trees Knoxville was officially formed in late 2015 and is now moving into its fourth year of working under its mission| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3041)|
| 0:50:48| to preserve, increase, and increase the urban tree canopy in the private and public lands of Knoxville and Knox County.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3048)|
| 0:50:55| And whereas, Trees Knoxville received a 501c3 status in March 2017| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3055)|
| 0:51:00| and has become a vital bridge between the citizens of Knox County and all activities involving trees across the county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3060)|
| 0:51:05| And whereas, since its formation in 2015, Trees Knoxville has commendably accomplished the following.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3065)|
| 0:51:11| Worked with 14 schools to plant a total of 138 trees on school grounds by 398 volunteers,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3071)|
| 0:51:17| trained 112 individuals through a 12-hour course on tree maintenance and care,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3077)|
| 0:51:22| donated over 2,000 trees to Knox County families,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3082)|
| 0:51:25| distributed thousands of trees to Knox County citizens through the Tennessee Environmental Council's annual 250K event,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3085)|
| 0:51:31| helped plant 112 street trees with grant funding from the Tennessee Division of Forestry,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3091)|
| 0:51:36| and an additional 54 street trees in cooperation with the City of Knoxville Urban Forestry Program,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3096)|
| 0:51:41| and planted 235 trees in city and county parks.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3101)|
| 0:51:44| And whereas, the Knox County Commission desires to recognize and congratulate Trees Knoxville for its accomplishments| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3104)|
| 0:51:50| and receipt of the Urban and Community Forestry Partnership Award from the Southern Group of State Foresters.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=3110)|

| 1:09:07| The Knox County Air Pollution Control Board| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4147)|
| 1:09:10| is an entity that was established in the ordinance,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4150)|
| 1:09:14| and the powers of the board are basically two.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4154)|
| 1:09:18| The first is whenever we develop regulations for our industry| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4158)|

| 1:09:41| and we typically will present that to them.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4181)|
| 1:09:44| The second is they are an appeal board.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4184)|
| 1:09:47| So if somebody disputes one of our enforcement actions we're taking| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4187)|
| 1:09:52| or a permit indecision,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4192)|

| 1:16:01| the person who receives the least votes will drop, and then it will go to two.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4561)|
| 1:16:05| Unless you get six on the first round.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4565)|
| 1:16:08| Correct.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4568)|
| 1:16:09| Yep.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4569)|
| 1:16:10| Correct.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4570)|
| 1:16:11| So, briefly, this is directly from our county commission rules.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4571)|
| 1:16:16| Nominators may speak directly about their nominee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4576)|
| 1:16:19| Nominees may speak about themselves.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4579)|
| 1:16:21| Hearing you guys talking.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4581)|
| 1:16:24| After each commissioner has afforded ample opportunity to express his or her views and responding views,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4584)|
| 1:16:29| the chair will ask if all commissioners are ready for a vote.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4589)|
| 1:16:31| If any commissioner wants further discussion, further discussion will be permitted.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4591)|
| 1:16:35| When discussion is complete, voting will commence.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4595)|
| 1:16:37| By roll call vote, each commissioner may vote in favor of one nominee by name,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4597)|
| 1:16:41| and the nominee with the least number of votes is disqualified.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4601)|
| 1:16:44| After each vote, the chair will invite further discussion by commissioners regarding the remaining nominees.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4604)|
| 1:16:49| If there is a tie vote, the chair will invite the nominators and remaining nominees to speak again,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4609)|
| 1:16:53| and the chair will invite further discussion by commissioners.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4613)|
| 1:16:56| Voting will resume until a nominee receives the votes of a majority of the members of the commission eligible to vote on the appointment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4616)|
| 1:17:02| That's the basics of our process straight from the rule book of the Knox County Commission.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267190826?start=4622)|
